## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / nonlinear oscillators
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the equation of motion (acceleration) for a nonlinear harmonic oscillator. The acceleration dv_dt is determined by restoring forces (nonlinear functions of x), damping forces (functions of v and possibly x), and potential external driving forces (functions of t).

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (1 + c2 * x**2) (nonlinear damping)
- Driven harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (external periodic driving)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Quadratic-cubic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (asymmetric potential)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity-dependent damping)
- Coulomb + viscous damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v * Abs(v) (quadratic damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-modulated stiffness)
- Helmholtz oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * v (quadratic nonlinearity with damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xтБ╡) тЖТ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power restoring forces (x┬▓) тЖТ asymmetric potential wells causing asymmetric oscillation
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v тЖТ energy dissipation or injection (damping/anti-damping)
- Position-velocity coupling terms like x┬▓*v тЖТ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of Van der Pol type systems
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) тЖТ external periodic driving forces causing resonance phenomena
- Cubic position term x┬│ with sign opposite to linear term тЖТ hardening or softening spring (Duffing-type behavior)
- Product of time-periodic function and position x*cos(c*t) тЖТ parametric excitation leading to parametric resonance
- Odd powers of velocity (v┬│) тЖТ nonlinear damping that limits cycle amplitude in self-excited oscillators
- Absence of explicit time dependence тЖТ autonomous system where phase portrait fully characterizes dynamics
